If there are more than four creators, click on the [More input rows] button.    If the work has been created by a named group rather than individuals, please fill in the 'Organisational creators'' instead.</td>

			<td style="border-top: 1px solid #000000; border-bottom: 1px solid #000000; border-left: 1px solid #000000; border-right: 1px solid #000000" align="left" valign="middle"><font face="courier new">text</font></td>

Example: Education Queensland. Please put funding bodies and sponsorship in the <span class="spCh spChx2018">&#x2018;</span>Funders<span class="spCh spChx2019">&#x2019;</span> field. </td>
			<td align="left"><br/></td>
		</tr>
